 What happened in the morning hearing? As soon as the court started hearing in the morning, Chief Justice Ranjan Gogoi gave some documents to CBI Director Alok Verma's lawyer Fali Nariman and asked him to read it as a senior lawyer
 court ne fali nariman se poocha ki jo baaten alok verma ke jawaab main hai, vahi chijen baahar kaise ain

 yani court ne is maamle main bahut kii ehtiyaat baratane ke aadesh die the

 The verdict has been reached in the famous Batla House encounter case that took place in Delhi five years ago
 dilli kii saket court ne kaha he ki encounter farji nahin tha
 At the same time, the court has held the only suspected terrorist Shahzad alias Pappu arrested in this case guilty of the murder of Inspector Mohan Chandra Sharma
 ab somvaar ko sajaa par bahes hogi
 Read: India Today's cover story on Batla House encounter convicted Shahzad under sections 302, 307, 186 and 120B of IPC
 court ne kaha ki shahzad ne goli markar inspector mohan sharma kii hatya kii
 Not only this, he also opened fire on the rest of the policemen and also tried to kill the head constable Balwant Singh
 udhar, shahzad ke gharavaalon ne kaha he ki court ke faisle se naakhush hai
 He says he has been implicated
 uske chachaa ne kaha he ki ve ab hoicourt main apil karenge
 Five years ago on 19 September 2008, an encounter took place at Batla House in Jamia Nagar area, in which two terrorists were killed
 dilli police ke ek jaanbaaj inspector mohan chandra sharma bhi shahid hue the
 The Delhi Police claimed at the time that it had intercepted the conspirators of the serial blasts in Delhi that same month, while some said the encounter was fake
 lekin ab court kaa yah faisla dilli police ke liye badi raahat lekar aayaa he
 This decision has dismissed the questions about the encounter
 apni chargeshit main police ne kaha tha ki us muthbhed ke dauraan shahzad apane dost junayd ke saath balakani se kudakar faraar ho gaya tha
 The police had said that all these terrorists were from the Indian Mujahideen terrorist organization, which were involved in the Ahmedabad and Delhi blasts, and they were planning to carry out further blasts in Delhi
 is encounter main dilli police ne mohan chandra sharma jaisaa apana ek jaanbaaj sipaahi bhi khoyaa, lekin iske baad bhi yah encounter kaaphi sawaalon ke ghere main bhi rahaa samay-samay par kuch logon ne ise phek encounter kehane main bhi der nahin kii
 The court had on July 20 reserved its order after the final cross examination of the police and the defense
 sunwaayee ke dauraan, shahzad ne 26 july 2008 ko ahmedabad main hue shrinkhalabaddh visphoton ke sambandh main vahaan kii sabarmati jail main band saf or jishaan ko bachaav paksh ke gavaahon ke taur par bulaakar daawa kiya tha ki vah maukey par nahin tha
 The prosecution had questioned 70 witnesses, including six eyewitnesses involved in the guerrilla squad of the special branch of the Delhi Police

 bharat main ek badi puraani kahawat he

 pakistan ke saath china is kahawat ko thodaa badalakar istemaal karata he

 pichley 18 saalon se
 
 yani 2001 ke sansad hamalon se 2019 ke pulavama hamale tak
 This dreaded terrorist of Pakistan has given many wounds to India one after the other
 duniya ke tamaam deshon ne mana kii jaish kaa ye sargana puri insaaniyat ke liye khatra he

 magar pichley 10 saalon se china aatank ke is sargana kii dhaal bana baitha he

 laga is baar to masood ko uske kiye kii sazaa mil hi jaaegi

 jis par america ne china se guzarish kii thi ki wo samajhadaari se kaam len
